1b1(phal chen): / 'phags pa sangs rgyas palnga po che zhes
1b2(phal chen): bya ba dra bam po drug cu rtsa ni/ gsum pa// / de nas byang
1b3(phal chen): chub sems dpe'i tshogasachen po de'i nang nas/ byang
2a1(phal chen): chub sems dpa' kha cig 'di snyam du sems te/ sangs rgyas
2a2(phal chen): b com ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi
2a3(phal chen): de khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sngon gyi smon lam dang / 'byung ba rnam
2a4(phal chen): par dag pa ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
2b1(phal chen): rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdung ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas
2b2(phal chen): skye ba ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku ni ji tsam zhig tu
2b3(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi
2b4(phal chen): khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes ni ji tsam zhig tu bsami gyis mi khyab/ sangs
2b5(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs
3a1(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa mi mnga' ba'i rnam par spyod pa ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas
3a2(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi khyab snyam pa dang / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis
3a3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' de dag gi sems thugs kyis thugs su chud nas/ byang chub sems dpa' ut+pa la'i snying po sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis
3a4(phal chen): babini du brlabs so/ / sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyi byin dang ldan par mdzad do// de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od kyis snang bar mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi gzi
3a5(phal chen): brjid kyis yongs su rgyas par mdzad do/ / sangs rgyas kyi mi 'jigs pa la rab tu bzhag go/ sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa khong du chud par
3a6(phal chen): mdzad do/ / sangs rgyas kyi bdag nyid che ba nyid dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi yul rab tu rtogs par mdzad do// chags pa med pa'i rgyud 'byam klas pa la rab tu
3b1(phal chen): bzhag go/ / sangs rgyas thams cad gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa'i rigs rab tu rtogs par mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi tshul gyi gnas brjod du med pa la rab tu bzhag pa mdzad do//
3b2(phal chen): de nas byang chub sems dpa' ut+pa la'i snying pos chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa rig cing khong du chud pas/ chags pa med pa'i dbyings su bsgrubs pa'i yid dang / chos thams cad
3b3(phal chen): la bsgrubs pa med par gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / kun tu bzang po'i smon lam dang ldan pa'i yang dag par 'jug pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rjes su song ba'i sangs
3b4(phal chen): rgyas blta ba dang / snying rje chen pos lta ba'i sems can thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i go cha chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa'i yi dam dang / spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor rgyun chad pa med pa dang /
3b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi ye shes mngon par bsgrub pa skad cig gi cha shas la rnam par spyod pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sgo mthong ba mi zad pa dang / tha dad pa yang dag par shes
3b6(phal chen): pa'i rnam pa gzungs thams cad kyis snang bar byas pa dang ldan pas/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' pad+mo'i snying po la 'di skad ces smras so// kye rgyal ba'i sras
3b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni tshad med pa la rnam par spyod pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rnam par 'phrul pa chen po la rnam par spyod pa'o//
4a1(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sgras sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa thams cad la sku'i mtshan nyid thams cad rab tu brnyes pa'o// sangs rgyas
4a2(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba ni ting nge 'dzin dang dgongs pas sbyar ba'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa bzhi ni
4a3(phal chen): brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa shin tu ston pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la bsam gyis mi khyab par rnam par spyod pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom
4a4(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi gsung dang dbyangs ni tshad med pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis chos kyi dbyings thugs su chud pa ni brjod du med pa'o// sangs rgyas
4a5(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba ni thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis chos kyi dbyings thug su
4a6(phal chen): chud cing bstan pa ni bsgribs pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings mtha' dngong bus
4a7(phal chen): med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos rnam pa bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gzugs kyi sku rnam par dag pa ni/ rnyog pa med par rgyud thams cad du byung bas mtha' dang
4b1(phal chen): dbus med pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa med pa'i spyan ni/ chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi spyan mngon par sangs rgyas pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas
4b2(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa med pa'i snyan ni/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi sgra bsgribs pa med par thugs su chud pos mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
4b3(phal chen): kyi shangs kyi skye mched ni/ sangs rgyas kyi mnga' thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brnyes pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ljags shin tu ya
4b4(phal chen): pa ni/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du gsung gi dbyangs rjes su 'gro bas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku'i chod nyid ni/ sems can
4b5(phal chen): thams cad ma lus pa'i sems kyi rnam pa de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ba rnam par dmigs pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs
4b6(phal chen): kyi 'phrin las ni/ chos kyi sku dang tha mi dad cing dus gsum chags pa med par thugs su chud cing rnam par dag pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs
4b7(phal chen): rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa bsgrib pa mi mnga' ba la rnam par spyod pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang dang / rnam par 'phrul pa dang / cho 'phrul mi zad pa yang dag par ston pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o//
5a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rnam par dag pa ni/ brjod du med pa'i rgyan byin gyis brlabs pas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing
5a2(phal chen): nye bar nyon mongs pa med pa yang dag par bstan te/ bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par dmigs par mdzad pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
5a3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i khyad par dang / smon lam thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa ni/ rnam par rol pa'i ye shes kyi chos yongs su rdzogs te/ chos thams cad rdzogs par byang
5a4(phal chen): chub par bya ba la mtha' dang dbus med pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dra gra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings
5a5(phal chen): mtha' dang dbus med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams so/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi skad cig la
5a6(phal chen): ye shes kyis mngon par bsgrubs pa yang dag par bstan pa'o/ / bcu gang zhe na/ skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du dga' ldan gyi gnas nas 'pho ba yongs
5a7(phal chen): su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i tshe yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du mngon par
5b1(phal chen): 'byung ba yongs su bstan pa dang / skang cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du byang chub kyi shing drung du bzhugs shing mngon par 'tshang rgyab yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gaN+Di
5b2(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'dul ba'i sems can yongs su smin pa'i
5b3(phal chen): tshul ji lta ba bzhin du dus la bab par shes pas/ sangs rgyas bsnyen bkur ba yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du sems can ji ltar 'dul ba'i tshul
5b4(phal chen): bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa brjod du med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi sku sna tshogs rnam par dmigs pa yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rgyan sna tshogs
5b5(phal chen): dang / rgyan brjod du med pas de bzhin gshegs pa'i khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i mdzod yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams
5b6(phal chen): thams cad du rnam par dag pa gcig ma yin pa thams cad yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar
5b7(phal chen): byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye ba thams cad du dbang po dang brtson 'grus rnam pa tha dang byung ba dang / mos pa dang spyod pa rnam pa tha dad pa byung ba la dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi chung ngu mngon par
6a1(phal chen): 'tshang rgyab yongs su bstan pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi skad cig la ye shes mngon par bsgrub
6a2(phal chen): pa yang dag par bstan pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi dus las mi 'da' ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas
6a3(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams mngon par 'tshang rgya ba ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi dge ba rnam par smin pa dang / rnam par ma smin
6a4(phal chen): pa mnyam pa nyid ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis yongs su smin pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams lung bstan pa ni de'i dus las mi
6a5(phal chen): 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sems can gyi bsam pa'i rgyud du cho 'phrul yongs su bstan pa ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/
6a6(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sems can mos pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa'i tshul bzhin du sku yongs su bstan pa ni de'i dus las mi 'das mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas
6a7(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams btang snyoms su bzhugs pa ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams yul dang / grong dang / grong rdal du gshegs pa
6b1(phal chen): ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dad pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa'i tshul bzhin du sems can yongs su 'dzin pa ni de'i dus las mi 'dra'
6b2(phal chen): bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can kun nas nyon mongs pa dang ldan zhing gdul dka' ba la gzhan la ltos pa mi mnga' bar 'dul ba ni de'i dus las mi
6b3(phal chen): 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pas rnam par 'phrul pa bstan pa ni de'i dus las mi 'dar bas dus la
6b4(phal chen): bab pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi dus las mi 'da' bru'o// kye rgyal ba'i skyes bcu po 'dings
6b5(phal chen): ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi yul dpe med cing bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par skyil mo krung gcig gis
6b6(phal chen): rgyas par dgang ba dang / dus gcig tu sangs rgyas thams cad yongs su bstan pa dang / 'od zer gcig gis 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad snang bar bya ba dang / sku gzugs
6b7(phal chen): gcig gis lus dang gzugs thams cad yongs su bstan pa dang / gnas gcig na bzhugs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par byon pa'i skur 'gyur ba dang / ye shes
7a1(phal chen): gcig rtogs pas chos thams cad la bsgribs pa med par 'gyur ba dang / thugs gcig bskyed pas chos kyi dbyings thams cad ma lus par rgyas par 'gengs pa
7a2(phal chen): dang / sangs rgyas kyi che ba nyid tshad med pa dang ldan pa'i gshegs stabs gcig gis de kho na nyid yang dag par bstan pa dang / dus gsum thams cad sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang gis rgyas
7a3(phal chen): par 'gedra ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad dang mi 'dres par bzhugs shing / 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang mi dmis pa'i
7a4(phal chen): tshul gyis rgyud kyi tshul gcig pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi yul dpe med cing bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o//
7a5(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlab sa mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'jug pa med pa'i chos thams cad
7a6(phal chen): la 'jug pas smon lam mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / lus med pa la lus mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad mi gnyis pa la mngon par 'tshang rgyab mngon par
7a7(phal chen): sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / sems can gyi mthar thug par bdag med pa la sems can 'dul ba mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad mtshan ma med pa la mtshan ma sna chos
7b1(phal chen): mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi yul ma skyes pa la 'jig rten gyi khams 'ju ba dang 'jig pa mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / yul thams cad mngon par
7b2(phal chen): 'du bya ba med pa la las kyi rnam par smin pa mngon sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad brjod du med pa la chos kyi dbyings su gsung ma ngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad
7b3(phal chen): kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang bas 'jug pa med pa la kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad ma skyes pa la skye ba dang
7b4(phal chen): 'jig pa'i mtshan nyid rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mngon par
7b5(phal chen): bsgrub pa'i ye shes so/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshad med pa khongs su chud pa dag ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas
7b6(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku ni dus gsum thams cad kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can thams cad 'dul bar mdzad pa ni tshe
7b7(phal chen): 'phrul chen po gsum gyi khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams tshig rab tu dbye ba thams cad la mkhas pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi gzungs thams cad kyi khongs su chud ba yin/
8a1(phal chen): @sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi 'khor lo thams cad ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa bzhir khongs su chud pa yin
8a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can thams cad yongs su mi gtong ba ni thugs rje chen po'i khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams rtag tu mnyam par gzhag
8a3(phal chen): pa ni dus thams cad du sems can thams cad la rnam par gzigs pa'i khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi dge ba'i rtsa bar ni sems can rnam
8a4(phal chen): par 'dul ba thams cad khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa mi mnga' bar spyod pa ni chos kyi dbyings thams cad khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom
8a5(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi skad cig gcig tu ni 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye bo thams cad khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi nyi
8a6(phal chen): ma gcig tu ni dus gsum gyi bskal pa'i grangs khongs su chud par bstan pa thams cad khongs su chud pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshad
8a7(phal chen): med pa'i khongs su chud pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba rnam te/ bcu gang zhen
8b1(phal chen): bdud kyi dkrugs ma rab tu 'joms shing rnam par 'thor ba ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o/ / mu stegs can gzhan dang bas
8b2(phal chen): kyi rgol ba tshar bcad pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o/ / 'dul ba'i sems can thams cad rab tu tshim par mdzad pa ni sangs rgyas
8b3(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o/ / sems can 'dul ba'i dbang gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gshegs pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
8b4(phal chen): rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o/ / chos kyi dbyings thugs su chud pa'i ye shes ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka'
8b5(phal chen): ba'o/ / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par skus khyab cing / sangs rgyas kyi sku rnam par phye ba sna tshogs thams cad du mi gnyis pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
8b6(phal chen): kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o/ / gsung gi yan lag thams cad la sems can mos par bya ba dang / thos par bya ba dang / gdul bar bya ba don yod par tha dad pa yang dag par
8b7(phal chen): mkhyen pa thog pa med pas bstan pa'i tshul du tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa bzhi 'byung ba ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// sangs rgyas
9a1(phal chen): @bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ba spu'i bu ga gcig nas de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed bsam gyi mi khyab cing / thogs pa med pa'i
9a2(phal chen): tshul du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi thabs kyis 'byung zhing / de bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi sku'i ba spu'i bu ga tham cad nas 'byung ba ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
9a3(phal chen): rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o/ / de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi
9a4(phal chen): khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yongs su ston cing / sangs rgyas kyi rgyan dang / rang bzhin gyi lhab lhub dang / chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba rgyun mi 'chad cing sems can rnam par 'dul ba thogs
9a5(phal chen): pa med la/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag tu gtogs pa rnams la'ang mi bde ba dang gnod pa med kyang rdul shin tu phra ba de'ang yangs par ma byas/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag kyang chung bar ma byas
9a6(phal chen): par ji ltar gnas pa'i chos kyi dbyings kyang thugs su chud pa'i ye shes mnga' ba ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// mun pa med pa'i khams
9a7(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pas mngon par sangs rgyas te/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la mun pa med cing bslabs pa mi mnga' la/ sems can pha rol gyi bsgribs pa sna tshogs kyi gnas par
9b1(phal chen): sel na/ de la bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang ldan pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos la bzod par dka' ba ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras
9b2(phal chen): bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos la bzod par dka' ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
9b3(phal chen): bdag nyid che ba rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu dag pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis yang dag par bsgrubs pa bdag nyid che ba ni/ sngon gyi mtha'
9b4(phal chen): nas rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing rnam par dag pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi rgyud du rigs dang ldan
9b5(phal chen): par 'byung ba'i bdag nyid che ba ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs rnam par dag pas rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
9b6(phal chen): ni rnam par shes pa la mi gnas pa ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug par gnas pas rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam
9b7(phal chen): par dag pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dus gsum la mi gnas par rnam par spyod cing chos thams cad la rten pa yang dag par bcom pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
10a1(phal chen): bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dngos po rnam pa tha dad pa la rnam par gzhag
10a2(phal chen): pa gcig gis len pa med pasdu/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid rje ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
10a3(phal chen): rnams ni sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mthar chos kyi dbyings la gnas pas mnyam pa'i bsod nams mi zad pa dang ldan pas mi zad pa'i bsod nams mnga' ba ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
10a4(phal chen): rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku gzugs dang kha dog mtha' yas pas/ 'jig rten
10a5(phal chen): gyi khams thams cad na sems can 'dul ba'i dus dang dbang gis chags pa med par bzhugs pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing
10a6(phal chen): shin tu rnam par dag pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mi 'jigs pa bzhi brnyes pas bag tsha ba mi mnga' bar bzhugs shing khyu mchog dang seng ge'i nga ro 'byin te/ rgol ba'i nang na stag lta
10a7(phal chen): bu'i mthu dang ldan la/ chos thams cad bstan pa la thugs sgron ma lta bu mnga' bas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam
10b1(phal chen): par dag pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni yongs su mya ngan las 'das nas bskal pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa zhig lon yang / mtshan gyi tshig thos pa tsam gyis bzhugs pa
10b2(phal chen): dang 'dra bar sems can rnams kyi yon shin tu sbyong zhing / mya ngan las 'das nas de srid kyi yun ring po 'das kyang sangs rgyas la bskyed pa'i yon zad par mi 'gyur bas/ sangs rgyas kyi bdag nyid che ba
10b3(phal chen): ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dag na bzhugs shing / 'jig
10b4(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgyang ring po na bzhugs kyang / 'jig rten gyi khams 'di na gnas pa'i sems can rnams kyis rjes su dran par byas na sku mngon par ston pa mdzad pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam
10b5(phal chen): kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams
10b6(phal chen): cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rnam par dag pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs
10b7(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ sangs rgyas kyi tshangs pa'i spyod pa rnam par dag pa la/ sngon gyi smon lam gyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chags pa med
11a1(phal chen): pa'i tshul khrims kyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa sel bas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/
11a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing gis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'khor gyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom
11a3(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni rigs rnam par dag pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni gzugs kyi sku'i mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po rnam par dag pas shin tu rnam
11a4(phal chen): par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi sku rnyog pa med pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi phung po
11a5(phal chen): bsgribs pa med pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa thams cad la mthu chen po brnyes shing / pha rol tu phyin pa dam pa brnyes pas shin tu
11a6(phal chen): rnam par dag pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas
11a7(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mdzad pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'byung zhing dus thams cad du gnas pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa'i thob pa'i sem can rnams la dus thams cad du
11b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bstan pa dang / sems can sems cad shes dang ldan pa rnams la dus thams cad du chos bstan pa dang / sems can sangs rgyas la dad pa'i sems dang ldan pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba dus thams
11b2(phal chen): du bskrad pa dang / chos kyi skyon med par 'das pa'i sems can rnams dus thams cad du ye shes khongs su chud par bya ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa dus
11b3(phal chen): thams cad du rgyun mi 'chad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du dus thams cad du chags pa mi mnga' bar gshegs pa dang / sems can thams cad
11b4(phal chen): la thugs rje chen po dus thams cad du mi gtong ba dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa dus thams cad du thogs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan
11b5(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs dus thams cad du thogs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos kyi dbyings gnas pa'i sangs rgyas dus thams
11b6(phal chen): cad du 'byung ba ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag nI/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mdzad pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'byung zhing dus thams cad du gnas pa'o//
11b7(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'i tshul rnams te/ bcu gang
12a1(phal chen): zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i skus ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin
12a2(phal chen): las tshad med pa brnyes pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi spyan gyi yul mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan
12a3(phal chen): 'das rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa ba tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi char mngon par 'bebs pas ye shes
12a4(phal chen): rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi yon tan dang legs pa mang po mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam
12a5(phal chen): nisngon gyi mtha'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i smoni lam dang khyad par mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni phyi ma'i mtha'i mur 'gro ba thams cad
12a6(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las rgyun mi 'chad par sgrub pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi rigs thams cad ma lus pa'i sems dang
12a7(phal chen): spyod pa la ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thams cad mkhyen pa'i bsod nams zil gyis mi non pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras
12b1(phal chen): bcu po de dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes rgya mtshom zad pa'o// kye dz+hal bu'i sras bcu po 'di dgam/
12b2(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi tshul rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad kyis mngon par byung ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan
12b3(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no/ / 'di lta ste/ chos thams cad la mi mkhyen pa gang yang mi mnga' ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/ thams cad kyang
12b4(phal chen): thugs rje chen po dang ldan pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no/ / 'di lta ste/ thams cad kyang stobs bcu tshad med pa dang ldan pa 'dri ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
12b5(phal chen): rnams kyi tshul yin no/ / 'di lta ste/ thams cad kyang bla na med pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/ thams cad
12b6(phal chen): kyang sems can 'dul ba yang dag par zhugs pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no/ / 'di lta ste/ thams cad kyang 'gro ba thams cad kyi don du mngon par sangs rgyas
12b7(phal chen): pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no/ / 'di lta ste/ 'dul ba'i sems can rnams 'dul ba la thogs pa mi mnga' ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul
13a1(phal chen): yin no/ / 'di lta ste/ mi gnyis par yang dag par spyod pa'i mtshan nyid kyi chos la rab tu gzhol ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no//
13a2(phal chen): 'di lta ste/ ji ltar yongs su smin par gyur pa dang dul bar gyur pa'i sem bral sangs rgyas kyi yul mu med pas/ sangs rgyas kyi yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa ston pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
13a3(phal chen): rnams kyi tshul yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi tshul lo// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di
13a4(phal chen): dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos mtha' yas pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgo rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sema?
13a5(phal chen): can gyi khams shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi spyod pa sna tshogs shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas
13a6(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad kyi las dang rnam par smin pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yos pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams
13a7(phal chen): cad la gdams ngag dang man ngag shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can mtha' yas pa rnam par sbyong ba'i nan tan gyi sgor mtha' yas/
13b1(phal chen): pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byung chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad la gdams ngag dung mun ngag gis yongs su gnog pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// s+yAngs rgyas bcwom lda
13b2(phal chen): 'das rnams ni byang chub sems dpa'i khyad par gyi smon lam rnam pa tha dad pas 'byung ba shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi kham
13b3(phal chen): thams cad ma lus pa'i 'du ba dang 'jig pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pa ni byang chub sems
13b4(phal chen): dpa'i bsam pa dang mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du 'das
13b5(phal chen): pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa ni bskal pa yangs pa de dang de dag tu bstan cing brjod pa dang / yongs su bshad pas sangs
13b6(phal chen): rgyas kyi ye shes thams cad khong du chud par bya ba'i sgor mtha' yas pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos mtha' yas
13b7(phal chen): pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgo'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sems can rnams la
14a1(phal chen): sgrub pa ste/ bcu gang zhen/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku yongs su bstan pa ni sems can rnams la spangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub bo// sangs rgya
14a2(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub bo/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams len pa mdzad pa'ang sems can rnams la sangs
14a3(phal chen): rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub bo/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams len pa mi mdzad pa'ango sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub bo// sa dang / chu dang / me dang / rlung
14a4(phal chen): gis kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub bo/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byin gyi rlabs kyi yul dang mangs
14a5(phal chen): dmigs pa thams cad yul du mdzad pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub bo/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam kyi mtshan kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi
14a6(phal chen): 'phrin las sgrub bo/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni zhing la dmigs par mdzad pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan
14a7(phal chen): 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub bo/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mi gsung bar bzhugs
14b1(phal chen): pa'ang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sems can rnams la
14b2(phal chen): sgrub pa'o/ / // bam po drug cu rtsa bzhi pa// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can gyi gtso
14b3(phal chen): bo'i chos te/ bcu gang zhe na/ smon lam chen po la rab tu brtan zhing smon lam zhig pa mi mnga' bas ji skad du gsung ba de ltar mdzad cing gnyis su mi gsung ba 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i
14b4(phal chen): chos dang po'o/ / phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal pa thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la yon tan thams cad yongs su rdzogs par mdzad par rab tu brtson zhing / sgyid lug pa
14b5(phal chen): mi mnga' ba 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos gnyis pa'o/ / sems can 'dul bar 'gyur ba gcig cig gzigs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par
14b6(phal chen): gshegs shing / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gshegs pa la thags thogs med pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos gsum pa'o// zhe sdang ba'i sems can rnams la thugs rje chen pos
14b7(phal chen): snyoms pa dang / dad pa'i sems can rnams la thugs rje chen pos snyoms pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos bzhi pa'o// gang gi tshe bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang
15a1(phal chen): dag par zhugs nas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas kyi bar du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag
15a2(phal chen): par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur ro snyam du/ byang chub kyi sems mnyam pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos lnga pa'o// dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yang dag par bsgrub cing thams cad
15a3(phal chen): mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su bsngo bas 'jug go/ 'jig rten pa'i rgyud la ma yin pa 'di ni sem can gyi gtso bo'i chos drug pa'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rjes su bsngo na sangs rgyas kyis spyad pa'i
15a4(phal chen): sems su lus kyi las dang / ngag gi las dang / yid kyi las kyis slob cing / nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi spyod pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su bsngo ba med pas bla na
15a5(phal chen): med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par sangs rgyas pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos bdun pa'o/ / byang chub sems dpa'i sems rnam par dag cing 'od gsal la dngas pa/
15a6(phal chen): thams cad du snang zhing kun tu 'od 'byung ba/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la snang zhing thams cad du snyoms pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid yongs su rdzogs par byed pa 'di ni sems can
15a7(phal chen): gyi gtso bo'i chos brgyad pa'o/ / 'jig rten pa'i bde ba thams cad yongs su spangs te/ 'jig rten pa'i dga' ba thams cad la ma chags pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyis
15b1(phal chen): gos pa med pa'i smon lam thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyis 'jig rten thams cad bde ba thams cad dang ldan par byas te/ sdug bsngal dang spros pa thams cad rab tu 'jom pa 'di ni sems can
15b2(phal chen): gyi gtso bo'i chos dgu pa'o/ / sdug bsngal gyi mi bde ba thams cad nyams su ba ba ste/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi don du dka' thub kyis shin tu gdungs kyang sla bar sems bskyed pas/
15b3(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs yongs su bsrung ba dang ldan pa dang / stobs bcu'i sa'i bar du sangs rgyas kyi yul la mos pas mthar thug pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos bcu pa
15b4(phal chen): ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs
15b5(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa chags pa med pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus
15b6(phal chen): pa thams cad du gshegs pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad na bzhugs pas chags
15b7(phal chen): pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na bzhugs pa dang / bzhengs pa dang / bzhud pas chags pa mi mnga'
16a1(phal chen): bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du chos ston pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par
16a2(phal chen): spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad kyi dga' ldan gyi gnas na bzhugs kyang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin//
16a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha' dang / da ltar byung ba'i mtha' la chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod
16a4(phal chen): pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad tsam gyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor na bzhugs kyang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/
16a5(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems dang spyod pa la gzigs shing thugs kyi skad cig gcig la cho 'phrul chen po gsum gyis sems can
16a6(phal chen): rnam par 'dul yang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku gcig gis kyang tshad med bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rnam par
16a7(phal chen): spyod pa chen por rnam par spyod kyang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi khams 'byam klas pa ma lus pa thams cad
16b1(phal chen): du/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos ma lus pa thams cad kyi mthar thug pa bsam gyis mi khyab par ston cing gsung yang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras ba
16b2(phal chen): po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa chags pa med pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'od dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan
16b3(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po sna tshogs kyis rnam par
16b4(phal chen): brgyan pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung yan lag mchog dam
16b5(phal chen): pa drug cu dang ldan zhing yan lag lci ba rgyus yongs su bzung ba dang / rgya na brgya skyong du mas rab tu brgyan pa dang / dbyangs kyi yan lag mtha' yas mu med pas rnam
16b6(phal chen): par dag pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi don dang tshig dang / yi ge brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pas rab tu tshim par mdzad pa dang / bag tsha ba mi mnga' bas
16b7(phal chen): seng ge'i nga ro chen po sgrogs pa dang / 'jigs pa med pa chen pos bsnyengs pa mi mnga' bar gyur pa dang / chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad du sems can thams cad la thag
17a1(phal chen): cing bsal te khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / sems can bsam pa tha dad pa dang / dbang po tha dad pa rnam pa sna tshogs 'dul bar nye bar gnas pa 'di ni
17a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung gi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs kyi 'phrin las ni stobs bcus brgyan pa/
17a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin chen po thams cad kyi me tog shin tu rgyas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad kyi rgyan gyis shin tu brgyan cing bsgrubs pas chags pa med pa'i spyod
17a4(phal chen): yul dang ldan pa/ chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi la rab tu rten pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos gting med pa rab tu brnyes pa/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi rgyan du gyur pa/
17a5(phal chen): dus gsum gyi chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems can kun gyi sems dang spyod pa thams cad skad cig gcig dang ldan pa'i shes rab kyis rab tu mkhyen pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom
17a6(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs kyi rkyen mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'od zer bye ba brjod du med pa rab tu 'gyed par mdzad de/ 'od zer de dag re re la'ang 'od zer
17a7(phal chen): gyi 'khor gyi dra ba brjod du med pa dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'byam klas pa thams cad ma lus par snang bar byed cing / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud thams cad mun pa med par ston pa/ sangs rgyas
17b1(phal chen): skye ba dang mi 'bral bas sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las phyir mi ldog cing don yod pa/ sangs rgyas skye ba brjod du med pas gnas pa med pa rang bzhin rnam par dag cing kun tu snyoms par 'byung ba ste/
17b2(phal chen): 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'od zer gyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams bzhad mo 'dzum par ston na/ zhal gyi sgo nas 'od zer kha dog sna
17b3(phal chen): tshegs kha dog du ma dang ldan pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad snang bar byed pa/ sems can gyi khams tshad med grangs med bsam
17b4(phal chen): gyis mi khyab pa rnam par ston pa/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu rnam pa gzhan du mi 'gyur bar lung ston pa/ 'tho ba thams cad du shin tu gsal ba 'byung ste/ 'di ni
17b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bzhad mo 'dzum pa bstan pa'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi sku ni tshad med pa ste/ bsgribs pa med
17b6(phal chen): pas rnam par dag pa chos thams cad chags pa med pa nyid kyi mthar thug pa/ mtha' dang dbus med pa'i chos kyi dbyings la gnas pa/ 'jig rten thams cad dang ma 'dres pa/ 'jig rten
17b7(phal chen): thams cad dang 'dzi ba med pa/ 'jig rten thams cad kyi de kho na nyid la yang dag par zhugs pa/ 'jig rten thams cad las gyen du 'phags pa/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos kyis yang
18a1(phal chen): dag par spyod pa/ tshig gi lam dang bral ba/ brjod du med pa'i mthar phyin pa/ phung po dang / khams dang / skye mched dang bral ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas
18a2(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'od tshad med pa mnga' ba ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du 'od ma
18a3(phal chen): 'dres shing rgyan du ma dang ldan pa kha dog sna tshogs brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rgyan dang ldan pa/ 'od kyi snang ba kun tu thogs pa med cing thams cad du chags pa med pa/ 'od kyi
18a4(phal chen): dkyil 'khor bsgribs pa med pa tshad med pa'i mdzod du gyur pa/ 'od thams cad kyi 'byung gnas su gyur pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'od kyi rgyan mchog dam pa za na
18a5(phal chen): med pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni kha dog mtha' yas pa mnga' ba ste/ kha dog yid du 'ong ba mnga' ba'o// kha dog 'od gsal ba mnga' ba'o// kha dog
18a6(phal chen): tshad med pa mnga' ba'o/ / sems can gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad kyi bsam pa dang mos pa bzhin du rnam par dmigs pa'i kha dog mnga' ba'o// de ma yin pa'i kha dog gzhan
18a7(phal chen): khams gsum du gtogs pa thams cad zil gyi gnon pa'i kha dog mnga' ba'o/ / kha dog thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brnyes pas// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni kha dog bla na
18b1(phal chen): med pa mnga' ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi kha dog rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge bas shin tu rnam par dag pa ste/
18b2(phal chen): 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs dge ba rin po che'i 'byung gnas su gyur pa la shin tu byung ba'o// chos nyid kyi rnam pa
18b3(phal chen): thams cad du khyad par yod pa dang / khyad par med pa'i spyod pas rnam par dag pa'i rgyan gyi ye shes skye ba thams cad nang du gtogs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs
18b4(phal chen): bsgribs pa med pa'i rgyud rnam par dag pas 'jig rten gyi mi snyan pa thams cad kyis mi snyan pa brjod du med pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis dus kyi rigs
18b5(phal chen): dang rgyud rnam par dag pa'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byams pa chen po'i mthu dang rang bzhin gyi rgyan mnga' ba ste/ shin tu dang ba yongs su rtog
18b6(phal chen): pa'i rnyog pa mi mnga' ba sku'i 'phrin las yongs su bsal ba/ blta bas mi skyo ba thugs shin tu rnam par bsal ba/ thugs rje chen po mnga' ba/ 'gro ba thams cad skyob pa/ yon gyi
18b7(phal chen): gnas kyi dam pa bla na med pa yongs su 'dzin pa'i nang na thugs brtse ba can phon par mdzad pa/ sems can thams cad kyi don du ye shes chen po byin gyis brlabs te/ bsod nam chen po yong
19a1(phal chen): su 'phags pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing du gyur pa/ sems can rnams kyi yon tan dang ye shes kyi phung po thams cad rnam par 'phel bar
19a2(phal chen): mdzad pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi byams pa chen po dang // thugs rje chen po'i mthar thug pa'i bsod nams kyi rgyan mchog dam pa blan med pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras

19b6(phal chen): thams cad kyi rgyan yang dag par bstan pa dang / bskal pa grangs med par brjod kyang yi ge shin tu bstan pa zad mi shes pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad rgyan thams

20a1(phal chen): gyis brlab pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos bzhi pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan

22a1(phal chen): thams cad du 'dod pa'i longs spyod rgya chen po bgegs med pa thams cad 'byung bar bya ba la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas

22b7(phal chen): 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o/ / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// yon tan thams cad
23a1(phal chen): kyi 'byung gnas phun sum tshogs pa'i spyod pa yongs su dag pa rdzogs par sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o/ / sems can yongs su
23a2(phal chen): smin par bya ba dang 'dul ba yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o/ / sangs rgyas kyi mnga' 'gro ba thams cad kyis zil gyis gnon pa yongs su
23a3(phal chen): rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o/ / zhing yongs su dag par bya ba yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par
23a4(phal chen): 'tshang rgya'o/ / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// mtshan dang / dpe byad bzang po dang /
23a5(phal chen): gzugs kyi sku blta na don yod par yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang mnyam pa
23a6(phal chen): nyid yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya ste/ / sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las thams cad yongs su rdzogs par mdzad nas yongs su mya ngan
23a7(phal chen): las 'da'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su rdzogs pa tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o//
23b1(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thabs mkhas pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad byin gyis
23b2(phal chen): brlabs pa med cing spros pa thams cad med par yang thugs su chud la/ dge ba'i sgo nas sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi nas kyang shin tu ston cing brjod de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
23b3(phal chen): kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa dang po'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad la gzigs pa med cing phan tshun du mkhyen pa med do// ma bcings ma grol ba dang /
23b4(phal chen): gzung ba med cing bsal ba med de yongs su rdzogs pa med pa'ang thugs su chud la/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la mnga' dam pa'ang bsnyes te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos thams
23b5(phal chen): cad la mnga' sbyar ba de'ang yang dag pa de kho na nyid ma nor ba rnam pa gzhan du mi 'gyur ba dang / chos thams cad bdag gi med cing yongs su 'dzin pa med la/ de kho na nyid kyi mtha' las rnam par
23b6(phal chen): mi 'da' yang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mnga' chen pos chos kyi dbyings thams cad snang ba la'ang rab tu mkhyen pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi
23b7(phal chen): thabs mkhas pa gnyis pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mtshan ma'i mtha' thams cad mi mnga' ste/ mtshan ma thams cad dang mi 'grogs shing mtshan ma'i mngon par
24a1(phal chen): shes pa thams cad dang ma 'dres la/ de'i rang bzhin du ngo bo nyid med pa dang / ji ltar ngo bo nyid med pa'i sgra'i tshul thams cad thugs su chud kyang gzugs kyi
24a2(phal chen): mtshan ma'i sku gzugs rnam par dag pa grangs med pa dang / zhing gi mtshan ma dang / rnam par spyod pa'i mtshan ma zad mi shes pa rnam pa sna tshogs yang dag par bstan cing bshad pa'i ye
24a3(phal chen): shes kyi phung po mun pa med pa 'gro ba thams cad kyi sgron ma chen por gyur pas mun pa med pa'i snang ba ston pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs
24a4(phal chen): mkhas pa gsum pa'o/ / chags pa med pa'i mtha' ni sngon gyi mtha' yang ma yin/ phyi ma'i mtha' yang ma yin/ da ltar byung ba'ang ma yin te/ chos kyi dbyings su gnas pa ni 'das pa
24a5(phal chen): 'am/ ma 'ongs pa 'am/ da ltar byung ba'ang ma yin pas/ de bzhin nyid kyi mtshan nyid kyis 'byung ba med kyang sangs rgyas 'byung ba rnams kyi rigs tshad med pa'i phyir shin tu bstan pa
24a6(phal chen): brjod du med pas 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye ba'ang rab tu brjed cing kun tu gzigs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi yul gyis de bzhin du gzigs pa 'di ni/
24a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa bzhi pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku'i 'phrin las dang / gsung gi 'phrin las dang / thugs
24b1(phal chen): kyi 'phrin las kyi mngon par 'du mdzad pa'ang mi mnga' la/ yongs su blang ba mi mnga' bas bzhugs shing rnam par phye ba med pa'i mthar thug pa ste/ dor ba med pa'i chos kyi gnas
24b2(phal chen): kyi pha rol tu phyin la bgrang ba'i tshul las rnam par 'das kyang tshul grangs med pa'i mdzod du gyur cing / bgrang ba dang mngon par sgrub pa mtha' yas pa dang / 'jig rten pa dang
24b3(phal chen): 'jig rten las 'das pa sna tshogs tha dad pa'i grangs kyi tshul thugs su chud pa ye shes bsgribs pa med pas gzigs pa rnams te/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems
24b4(phal chen): can 'dul ba rnam par dmigs pa la rdzu 'phrul sna tshogs tshad med mu med par mngon par sgrub pa mdzad pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas
24b5(phal chen): pa lnga pa'o/ / chos thams cad lta ba med pas tha mi dad pa dang / bye brag med pa dang / 'byung ba med pa dang / mtshan nyid med pa dang / sna tshogs med pa dang / blang ba med pa dang /
24b6(phal chen): dor ba med pa dang / rang bzhin med par rab tu mkhyen kyang chos kyi rgyud shin tu nges pa yang dag par sgrub cing 'jig rten gyi tshul dang 'gal ba med pa dang / rang bzhin med pa'ang yang
24b7(phal chen): dag par gzigs pas thams cad mkhyen pa thams cad gzigs pa mkhyen par bya ba thams cad ma lus par gzigs pas chos la mnga' sbyar ba thams cad kyang rab tu ston la/ de bzhin nyid kyi rang bzhin las kyang mi nyams pa 'di ni/
25a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa drug pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom
25a2(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni thugs su chud pa'i rnam pa gcig gis gzhan dang gzhan mkhyen par bya ba/ chos de'i skyon med pa las rnam par ma 'das pa/ gnas pa med pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba
25a3(phal chen): rnam par dag pa/ mnyam pa nyid kyi chos kyi skyon med pas dus thams cad du gnas pa rab tu mkhyen te/ de la'ang nyi ma gcig gam/ zla ba phyed dam/ lo gcig gam/ lo brgya
25a4(phal chen): 'am/ bskal pa 'jig pa dang / 'du bas rjes su bsnyag pa dang / phyir phyogs pa mi mnga' bar dus tshad med pa dang / nyi ma gcig dang / yud tsam gcig gi dus dang /
25a5(phal chen): snga dro nas nyi ma phyed kyi dus dang / phyi dro nas snga dro'i dus dang / nyi ma gud nas phyi dro'i dus dang / nyi ma bgrangs pa'i dus dang / nyi ma bdun dang / zla ba phyed kyi dus dang / zla ba dang /
25a6(phal chen): lo dang / lo brgya'i dus dang / bskal pa gcig gi dus dang / tshad med grangs med pa bsam gyis mi khyam pa'i dus nas/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i dus su chos bstan pa dang
25a7(phal chen): chos kyi 'khor lo thogs pa med cing phyir mi ldog/ rgyun chad par mi 'gyur/ bral bar mi 'gyur/ bar chad par mi 'gyur/ med par mi 'gyur/ 'jig par mi 'gyur/
25b1(phal chen): g.yo bar mi 'gyur/ ring du mi 'gyur/ 'khor de na gnas pa nyi du'ang rgyun chad par mi 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa bdun pa'o// /
25b2(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad rtag du rus la bab par bzhugs pa ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mo 'jigs pa tshad med pa
25b3(phal chen): mnga' ba'o/ / tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa grangs med pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa tshad med pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa zad mi shes pa mnga'
25b4(phal chen): ba'o/ / tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa thogs pa med pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa mtha' yas pa mnga' ba'o// thun mong ma yin pa'i tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa
25b5(phal chen): mnga' ba'o/ / tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa mthar thug pa med pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa de kho na dang ldan pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa
25b6(phal chen): tshig gi tshul thams cad rab tu rtogs pa mnga' ba'o/ / chos thams cad tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa mnga' ba'o// bsam pa dang / mos pa dang / dbang po ji lta ba bzhin du
25b7(phal chen): chos kyi tshul dang rnam grangs tshul ji ltar rnam par bkod pa bzhin du sa mtshams med par ston te/ mdo sde bye ba khrag khrig brjod du med pa'i yang brjod pa med pa rnams mdo sde de dang
26a1(phal chen): de la thog ma dang / tha ma dang / dbus kyi tshul gyis yang dag par ston te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa brgyad pa'o// /
26a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni ming med kyang / ming dang rigs su byung ba'i chos thams cad tshig dang yi ges shin tu dbyangs pa'i dbyings mngon par sangs rgyas pa ste/ ming 'das
26a3(phal chen): pa ma yin pa dang / ming ma 'ongs pa ma yin pa dang / ming da ltar byung ba ma yin pa dang / ming sems can ma yin pa dang / ming zhing ma yin pa dang / ming chos ma yin pa dang /
26a4(phal chen): ming yon tan ma yin pa dang / ming byang chub sems dpa' ma yin pa dang / ming sangs rgyas ma yin pa dang / ming grangs ma yin pa dang / ming grangs med pa ma yin pa dang
26a5(phal chen): ming skye ba ma yin pa dang / ming 'gag pa ma yin pa dang / ming med pa ma yin pa dang / ming yod pa ma yin pa dang / ming gcig pa ma yin pa dang / ming tha dad pa ma yin pa
26a6(phal chen): dang / ming thams cad ma yin pa dang / chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis brjod du med pa dang / phyogs med pa dang / brda med pa dang / tshig gi lam med pa dang /
26a7(phal chen): sgra dang bral ba/ sgra'i rnam pa thams cad mi 'byung ba yongs su bsgrubs pa med pa/ byas pa dang rnam par byas pa med pa/ rnam pa gcig ma yin pa/ rnam pa mang po ma yin pa'ang
26b1(phal chen): thugs su chud la/ brjod pa dang spyad pa thams cad la'ang ba rol tu phyin pa'i mchog brnyes pa dag ste/ rnam par rtog pa'i yul mi mnga' ba dag go/ mngon par 'du mdzad pa med
26b2(phal chen): pa la rab tu brtson pa dag go/ rtog pa dang / kun tu rtog pa dang / yongs su rtog pa 'gag pa dag go/ spyod pa thams cad la mi klanas par spyod pa dag ste/ 'di ni sangs
26b3(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thatha mkhas pa dgu pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad kyi gzugs ma skyes pa rab tu mkhyen pa ste/ tshor ba'i
26b4(phal chen): spros pa med pa dang / 'du shes kyi zangs med pa dang / 'du byed kun tu rgyu ba med pa dang / rnam par shes pa nye bar len pa med pa dang / rang bzhin gyis zhi bar rab tu
26b5(phal chen): mkhyen te/ chos thams cad skye mched kyi rgyud med pa dang / khams rnams mi dmigs pa dang / chos thams cad mi 'jigs pa dang / chos thams cad bskyed du med cing
26b6(phal chen): rang bzhin gyis nam mkha' lta bu dang / chos thams cad dben pa dang / las med pa dang / rnam par smin pa med pa dang / spyod pas 'byung ba med pa dang / ma sgrub pa dang /
26b7(phal chen): ma byung ba dang / grangs kyis mi brjod pa dang / yod pa ma yin pa dang / med pa ma yin pa dang / ma skyes pa dang / ma 'gogs pa dang / kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa
27a1(phal chen): dang / rnam par byang ba med pa dang / skyon med pa dang / gnas pa med pa dang / yongs su gnas pa med pa dang / yongs su smin par byas pa med pa dang /
27a2(phal chen): rnam par btul ba med pa dang / sems can med pa dang / sems can med pa ma yin pa dang / srog med pa dang / srog med pa ma yin pa dang / rkyen med pa dang / rkyen med pa ma
27a3(phal chen): yin pa dang / rten pa med pa dang / rten pa med pa ma yin par chos thams cad thugs su chud kyang chos kyi dbyings thams cad shin tu bstan pa la pha rol tu phyin pa'i dam pa bsnyes pa dag ste/
27a4(phal chen): nges pa dang / ma nges pa dang / log par nges pa'i phung po gsum rnam par dgong ba rnams la stobs bcus thugs su chud pa'i ye shes mi 'jigs pa bzhis rnam par dag pa'i sangs rgyas
27a5(phal chen): kyi yul chen po dang ldan pas seng ge'i sgra sgrog pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa bcu pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de
27a6(phal chen): dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
27a7(phal chen): rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las rgya chen po tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams te/ de dag ni sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs ma gtogs par lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten
27b1(phal chen): dang 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis 'jug par mi nus pa'o// bcu gang zhe na/ phyogs bcu'i
27b2(phal chen): nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas gtugs pa'i chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du dga' ldan du skye ba bstan pa dang / byang chub sems
27b3(phal chen): dpa'i spyod pa mu med pa dag la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad de/ kha dog tshad med pa/ gzi brjid tshad med pa/ snang ba tshad med pa/ dbyangs tshad med pa/ dbyang
27b4(phal chen): kyi yan log rnam par dag pa tshad med pa/ gsung brjod pas rnam par dmigs pa tshad med pa/ ting nge 'dzin tshad med pa/ shes rab dang ye shes yul tshad med pa mnga' ba'i
27b5(phal chen): rnams lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten la phan 'dogs pa mdzad de/ bdud dang bcas pa/ tshangs pa dang bcas pa/ dge sbyong dang bram ze'i skye dgu dang bcas pa//
27b6(phal chen): lha dang / mi dang / lha ma yin du bcas pa'i 'jig rten la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// byams pa chen po'i spyod yul thogs pa med pa dang / thobs thugs rje chen
27b7(phal chen): po'i sgo mthar thug pas sems can la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do/ / bsod nams kyi stobs dang mnga' phun sum tshogs pa dang / dbang po rnam par sbyang ba dang /
28a1(phal chen): cang shes kyi sems yongs su dag pas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// theg pa sna tshogs rnam par dag pas kyang sems can rnams la
28a2(phal chen): phan 'dogs pa mdzad do/ / theg pa chen po yongs su rdzogs par bya bas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// 'gro ba thams cad gdon pas kyang sems
28a3(phal chen): can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las dang po'o// dga' ldan gyi pho zang nas 'phos pa med
28a4(phal chen): kyang yum gyi skur gshegs shing / byang chub sems dpa'i sku tha ma skye bar bstan pa/ sgyu ma lta bur yongs su spyod pa/ sprul pa lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin gyi mthar thug pa mig
28a5(phal chen): yor lta bur rnam par dmigs pa/ nam mkha'i yul tshad med par khyab pa/ bzhed pa bzhin du skye'ang chags pa mi mnga' ba/ smig rgyu ba lta bur bstan pa/ nyon mongs pa
28a6(phal chen): med pa'i chos la yang dag par gzhil ba/ gnas med pa'i ye shes la gnas pa/ rang bzhin gyis 'dod chag dang bral bas rnam par dag pa/ rgyan shin tu rgya che ba'i mdzod/
28a7(phal chen): kyis sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// khang pa brtsegs pa rin po che las byas pa'i pho zang chen po rin po che'i rgyan mang po ldan pa na bzhugs pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi 'dzin
28b1(phal chen): las mdzad do/ / rdzu 'phrul gyis kyang sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// yid la bya ba byin gyi rlabs chen pos kyang sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// rnam par 'phrul pa'i
28b2(phal chen): mdzod chen po yang dag par bstan pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do/ / ye shes kyi nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor chen pos kyang sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// yum sku skyed pa'i
28b3(phal chen): skra na bzhugs pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do/ / sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi spyod yul chen po bsnyes pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis 'dzi/
28b4(phal chen): rten byin du brlabs pa mtha' yas pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// ting nge 'dzin chen po grangs med pa la rnam par spyod cing snyoms par 'jug pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin
28b5(phal chen): las mdzad do/ / ting nge 'dzin las bzhengs pa de dang de dag gis kyang sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// spyod pa'i thog ma la yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa chen po'i mthar thug pa'i
28b6(phal chen): bar du thog ma dang / dbus dang / tha ma'i tshul gyis kyang sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// sa 'di la gnyis su med pa thams cad mthar phyin par byas nas tha mar 'jig rten gyi
28b7(phal chen): grangs kyis skye ba yongs su ston te/ skye bas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// gzhon nur gyur pas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin
29a1(phal chen): las mdzad do/ / byang chub sems dpar gyur pas kyang 'jig rten thams cad dus ng+yas rgyas kyi 'dzin las mdzad do// mngon par byung rab kyang 'jig rten pa
29a2(phal chen): cad du sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do/ / mngon par 'tshang rgyabs kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas kyang 'jig rten thams cad
29a3(phal chen): dusangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do/ / thabs mkhas pa sna tshogs kyis kyang 'jig rten sna tshogs/ 'jig rten tshad med pa/ 'jig rten kun tu mtha' yas pa/ phyogs
29a4(phal chen): kyi dra ba'i rgyud dang rigs thams cad kyi 'jig rten ma lus pa thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do/ / zhing gi rgyud ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do//
29a5(phal chen): las kyi rnam par smin pa ma lus pa'i 'dzin rten du sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// sems can gyi rgyud ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// skye ba dang
29a6(phal chen): shi 'pho ba'i rgyud ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do/ / sprul pa chen po'i rgyud dang / sangs rgyas kyi rigs dang / chos dran pa'i sgo'i 'khor los kyang sangs
29a7(phal chen): rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'drin las gnyis pa'o// dge bar spyod pa'i las rnam par dag cing / gdung rabs thams cad du
29b1(phal chen): ye shes kyi tshul rnam par dag par sku tshe'i rgyud kyi tshul dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad gdul ba thugs su chung ba/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongs su rdzogs par mdzad cing btsun mo'i
29b2(phal chen): 'khor gyi nang na bzhugs pa ston kyang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba'i tshul gyi gnas la bzhugs pa rnams sgra dang tshig thams cad dang bral bar brtag pas/ dngos po
29b3(phal chen): thams cad dngos po med pa las byung bar khong du chud par bya ba dang / dngos po thams cad shes pa la gzud par bya ba dang / tshul khrims thams cad thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi mthar thug par
29b4(phal chen): yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / snying rje chen pos 'gro ba mu med pa la rnam par blta bar bya ba dang / byams pa chen pos sems can med pa'i yul la rab tu rtog par bya ba dang / dga' ba
29b5(phal chen): chen pos 'jig rten brjod du med par khong du chud par bya ba dang / btang snyoms chen pos sems la dbang sgyur ba la gnas par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i yon tan gyis rang yongs su/
29b6(phal chen): rgyas par byed par bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi lus ma lus par mngon par bsgrub par bya ba dang / thams cad du gnas med pa'i lus yongs su rdzogs par byed par bya ba dang /
29b7(phal chen): 'khor thams cad rnam par dag par nan tan du byed par bya ba dang / chos bstan pa rnam par brjod pa rab tu brjod par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi dngos po la spod par bya ba dang / 'gro
30a1(phal chen): tha tham sa cad kyi nyes pa la tog par bya ba ma dzad cing spyod pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa bas rnam par smin pa yang dag par bstan pa dang / ji ltar bkod pa'i tshul du sems/
30a2(phal chen): can gdul ba dang / yongs su ma smin pa'i sems can yongs su smin par bya ba dang / yongs su sbyin pa rnams tshul bzhin du gdul ba dang / grangs med pa'i thabs mkhas pa mngon par
30a3(phal chen): bsgrub pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las phyir mi ldog pa yongs su bstan pa dang / sgo sna tshogs nas chos kyi spyod pa rab tu brjod pa dang / sems can rnams kyi bsam pa sna tshogs
30a4(phal chen): rnam par sbyang ba dang / thugs rje chen po las byung ba'i chos kyi sprin gyis mngon par spang ba dang / thams cad la skyob pa'i byams pa chen po bskyed pa'i cho 'phrul gsum gyis yongs
30a5(phal chen): su brlan pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad mthong ba dang / rnam par dmigs pa'i btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nang du bston pa yan chad du 'jig rten mtha' dang dbus med par sangs rgyas
30a6(phal chen): kyi 'phrin las yongs su bstan pa mdzad cing / ye shes kyi mthu chen po thogs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi mngon par mkhyen pa bsgribs pa med par bsgrubs pa dang /
30a7(phal chen): chos rnam pa gsum gyi thabs mkhas pa dang ldan pa'i 'phrin las kyi mtha' dang / sku'i 'phrin las kyi mtha' shin tu rnam par dag pa dang / gsung gi 'phrin las ye shes
30b1(phal chen): nyams pa med pas rnam par dag pa dang / thugs kyi 'phrin las kyi mtha' zab cing chags pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'i thabs la mkhas pas sems can rnams kyi don mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs
30b2(phal chen): rgyas rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las gsum pa'o/ / / bam po drug cu lnga pa/ rnam par rgyal ba chen po mnga' ba rnams ni btsun mo'i 'khor
30b3(phal chen): / rgyan rnam par phye ba tshad med pa dang ldan pa yid du 'ong ba spangs te/ mngon par 'byung ba'i spyod pa yongs su bstan pas sems can rnams 'jig rten gyi gnas las bskyod pa dang / 'jig
30b4(phal chen): rten gyi mngon par zhen pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / 'jig rten du gtogs pa thams cad mi rtag par shes par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi tshul la mngon par zhen pa rnam par bzlog pa dang /
30b5(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi dga' ba la sred pa yongs su bcad pa dang / 'jig rten nyon mongs pa byang zhing nub pa la yang dag par spyod par bya ba dang / sems can gyi don rjes su dran par bya ba'i phyir mngon par
30b6(phal chen): 'byung ba'i don la rab tu gzhol ba dang / khyim pa'i tshul yongs su spang ba bstan pa dang / nyon mongs pa med pa'i chos kyi sbyor ba la yang dag par gnas par bya ba dang / sngon gyi smon lam yongs
30b7(phal chen): su rdzogs par bya ba dang / yon tan gyi dkyil 'khor tshad med pa yongs su snang bar bya ba dang / ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor chen po bsnyes pas sems can rnams kyi mi shes pa'i sgrib pa rab tu
31a1(phal chen): bsal ba dang / bdag nyid bsod nams kyi zhing bla na med par gyur par 'gro ba thams cad la bstan pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad sangs rgyas la bskyed pa'i
31a2(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba'i nang du 'dus par 'gro ba thams cad la yang dag par brjod pa dang / bdag nyid kyis ye shes kyi don gzigs par bstan pa dang / sems can rnams rnam par dag pa'i sgor
31a3(phal chen): brjod pa dang / sems can rnams kha na ma tho ba med pa'i sgor sgrub pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad du 'byung ba'i sgo rab tu bstan pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rgyal mtshan yang dag
31a4(phal chen): par bsgreng ba mdzad cing mngon par 'byung ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las bzhi pa'o// don gcig ma yin pa mkhyen pa dang ldan pa thams
31a5(phal chen): cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi mthar thug pa rnams ni/ chos thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya bar bya'o zhes byang chub kyi shing drung du byon te/ byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya bas kyang bdud kyi
31a6(phal chen): dpung thams cad rab tu gzhom pa dang / sku'i byin gyi rlabs kyi mdzod kyis chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad du rgyas par dgang ba'i phyir/ byin gyi rlabs zad mi shes pa'i mthar thug pas
31a7(phal chen): mtha' rnam par spangs pa/ spyod pa tshad med pa rab tu brnyes pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i yul gyis rnam par rol pa'i ye shes kyi don dang ldan pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i yon tan yang
31b1(phal chen): dag par bsgrub pa yongs su rdzogs pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du gdan rnam par bkram pas yongs su rgyas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing ma lus pa thams cad du byang chub
31b2(phal chen): sems dpa' rnam par dmigs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dam pa thob pa rnams kyis zhal du blta ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i thams cad kyi rnam pa dang / smon lam khyad par can
31b3(phal chen): dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad kyis yang dag par bsam pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo zab mo rab tu bskor ba/ sangs rgyas kyi yul tshad med pa bsams
31b4(phal chen): pas byang chub sems dpa' brjod du med pa'i 'byung gnas su gyur pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa sna tshogs spyod pa la yang dag par gzhol ba'i byang chub sems dpa' 'khor gyi dkyil
31b5(phal chen): 'khor rnam par dag pa mnga' ba/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis byin du rlob pa'i yul mnga' ba/ dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa'i sems can gyis rnam par dmigra
31b6(phal chen): pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad tha mi dad pa dang ldan pa 'byung ba'i sa byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mtha' yas pa'i mthu'i gnas la yon tan gyi khyad par thams cad rab tu bskyes
31b7(phal chen): pas bzhugs pa/ 'jig rten gyi rnam pa thams cad ma lus pa'i mthar thug pa/ sems can gyi rnam pa thams cad dang / zhing gi rnam pa thams cad dang / chos
32a1(phal chen): kyi rnam pa thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam pa thams cad dang / yongs su smin par bya ba'i rnam pa thams cad dang / dus kyi rnam pa thams cad dang /
32a2(phal chen): 'dul ba'i rnam pa thams cad dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa'i rnam pa thams cad ma lus par mthar thug pa'i rnams 'gro ba ma lus pa thams cad du mos pa ji lta bzhin du rnam
32a3(phal chen): b.rar+ya 'tshang rgya bas/ sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin lus mdzad de/ 'di ni sang+yas kyis bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'dzin las lnga pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam
32a4(phal chen): kyi chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba mdzad pa phyir mi ldog pa'i tshul gyis phyir mi ldog pa'i 'khor lo dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyis khong du chud par 'gyur ba'i tshul gyis tshad med pa'i/
32a5(phal chen): 'khor lo dang / mi 'jigs pa'i seng ge'i nga ro chen po'i tshul gyis thams cad ma lus par mngon par sangs rgyas pa'i 'khor lo dang / chos kyi mdzod mun pa med pa'i sgos snang bar byed
32a6(phal chen): pa'i tshul gyis chos thams cad mkhyen pa'i mdzod kyi 'khor lo dang / ye shes nam mkha'i dbyings ltar tshad med pa'i tshul gyis chags pa med pa'i 'khor lo dang chos bam
32a7(phal chen): cad kyi dngos po med pa'i rang bzhin rab tu rtogs par bya ba'i tshul gyis bsgribs pa med pa'i 'khor lo dang / sems can thams cad kyi chos kyi mig rnam par sbyong ba'i tshul gyis
32b1(phal chen): 'jig rten thams cad kyi sgron ma'i 'khor lo dang / 'jig rten thams cad du rgyas par 'grengs pa'i tshul gyis thams cad mkhyen pa'i chos brjod pa'i 'khor lo dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos
32b2(phal chen): thams cad dang mi 'gal ba'i tshul gyis sangs rgyas thams cad 'dab 'dres par gyur pa'i 'khor lo dang / de dag la sogs pa rnam pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du chos kyi 'khor lo bskor
32b3(phal chen): bas sems can thams can gyi sems dang spyod pa'i rnam pa la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor te/ de ltar chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
32b4(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin la bsam gyis mi khyab po mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las drug pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
32b5(phal chen): ni grong dang / grong khyer dang / grong rdal dang / rgyal po'i gnas su gshegs pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad de/ mi'i rgyal po'i
32b6(phal chen): gnas dang / lha'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / klu'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / gnod sbyin gyi rgyal po'i gnas dang / dri za'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / lha ma yin gyi rgyal po'i
32b7(phal chen): gnas dang / nam mkha'i lding gi rgyal po'i gnas dang / mi 'am ci'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / lto 'phye chen po'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / srin po'i rgyal po'i gnas dang /
33a1(phal chen): sha za'i rgyal po'i gnas dag tu gshegs kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad de/ 'di lta ste/ grong khyer gyi
33a2(phal chen): sgor byon nas g.yo ba dang / 'od zer snang ba dang / long ba rnams mig 'thob pa dang / 'on pa rnams kyis sgra thos par 'gyur ba dang / smos pa rnams dran pa 'thob par 'gyur ba
33a3(phal chen): dang / gos med pa rnams gos 'thob par 'gyur ba dang / sdug bsngal ba rnams bde ba 'thob pa dang / rol mo'i cha byad ma dkrol ma brdungs par sgro yid du 'ong bar 'byin pa dang / rgyan snod
33a4(phal chen): na 'dug pa dang / gnas nas ma phog pa dang / ma bskyod ma dkrol bar bskyod cing dkrol ba'i sgra 'byung ba dang / bya sna tshogs mang po'i sgra skad yid du 'ong ba 'byung ba dang / lta na
33a5(phal chen): gtang mi phra zhing mi mthun pa med pa'i sku mthong bas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// mtshan dang dpe byang
33a6(phal chen): bzang po bstan pas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad de/ yongs su gzigs pa dang / rnam par
33a7(phal chen): gzigs pa dang / brkyang ba dang / bskum pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// gshegs pa dang / slar bzhud pa dang / bzhengs pa
33b1(phal chen): smra sa smra s
33b2(phal chen): ems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do/ / rdzu 'phrul gyi cho 'phrul dang / yongs su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul drung / rjes su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul gyis kyang / sangs rgyas
33b3(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams 'jig rten gyi khams kyi yul sems can bsam pa sna tshogs rgya mtsho dang ldan pa/ 'jig rten gyi spyod pa thams cad rgyu zhing 'byung ba dang ldan pa/ dge ba'i rtsa
33b4(phal chen): bachen pos shin tu bstan pa/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa dang ldan pa/ sngon 'grogs 'grogs pa byang chub sems dpa' dang gnas pa'i sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las
33b5(phal chen): mdzad do/ / yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams ni sku gzugs blta na mi ngoms pa'o zhes bya bar gzhol ba dang / sangs rgyas rnams skye bar dkon no// zhes bya bar yid
33b6(phal chen): ches par byed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa mthong zhing de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung thos pa ni bsod nams kyi chos dkar po'i 'byung gnas su gyur pa'o// zhes sangs rgyas kyi
33b7(phal chen): spyod pa yid la byed pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad rnam par dag pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa skye ba yin no zhes bya bar khong du chud par byed pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi yon
34a1(phal chen): tan bsngags pa ni mtha' yas pa'o zhes bya bar yang dag par lta ba dang / ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas 'byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs yang dag par bsgrub
34a2(phal chen): pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba dang mos pa'i tshul thams cad kyis sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mnyes par byed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams ni yon tan mtha' yas pa'o zhes
34a3(phal chen): khong du chud par byed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa ni sems can thams cad la mngon du gyur par rtog pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa ni sems can gyi rigs bsam gyis mi khyab
34a4(phal chen): pa'i gnas su gyur par sems pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa ni zhing thams cad na snang bar khong du chud pa dang / de lta bu'i dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad 'byung bas
34a5(phal chen): 'jig rten thams cad na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do/ / dad par byas pa dang / phyag 'tshal ba dang / thal
34a6(phal chen): mo sbyar ba byas pa dang / rjes su bstod pa dang / spyan drangs pa dang / mchod pa dang / mngon du mthong ba dang / 'dzum pa byas pa dang / sangs rgyas la dga'
34a7(phal chen): ba'i sems kyis mos par byas pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba'i sgo nas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// sangs rgyas
34b1(phal chen): rjes su dran par gyur pas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// sangs rgyas mthong bar 'dod par bya bas
34b2(phal chen): kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku kha dog dang dbyibs kyi rnam pa tshad med

34b5(phal chen): 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las rnam pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa dag 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa dang / /

34b7(phal chen): pa dang / bsam pa la gnas pa dge ba rgya che ba tshad med pa dag phyir mi ldog pa'i yul dang / snying rje chen po rab tu bskul ba dang / sngon gyi smon lam gyis yong su skyo ba me/
35a1(phal chen): pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mkhyen pa'i stobs dang shugs kyis 'jig rten thams cad du 'byung ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams

35a5(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las gzhan gyis mi tshugs pa'i ye shes dang / smon lam gyi tshul gyis mos pa bzhin du 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la rgyun mi 'chad par

36b1(phal chen): mtha' lta bur sems can rnams kyis shes par bya ba dang / sems can rnams kyis 'jig rten thams cad du dga' bar bya ba med par bstan pa dang / sems can rnams la ma byon pa'i sangs
36b2(phal chen): rgyas gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa mnyes par gyis shig par bstan pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba bstan du mi rung bar khong du chud par bya ba

36b5(phal chen): sems la byin gyis brlab par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas la dmigs pa'i rkyen 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad phyin par dgongs pa mdzod pa dang / skra thams cad bshig/

37a1(phal chen): rnams kyi sangs rgyab kyi 'phrin las dgu pa'o/ / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams mya ngan las 'da' ba'i rtse 'jig rten thams cad na sems/
37a2(phal chen): can rnams smre sngags 'don cing ngu ba dang / mya ngan byed pa dang / mchi ma 'byin pa dang / yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas she 'am/ thugs rje chen po zhe 'am//

37b6(phal chen): par phye ste/ sku gdung dang ring bsrel tshad med pa/ grangs med pa/ dpag tu med pa/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa byin gyis rlob bo// de bzhin

38a1(phal chen): dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po'i gnas dang / mi'i gnas dang / srin po'i gnas dgra/
